<script>\n
 window.Flux = {\n
 applyAppearance (appearance) {\n
 let applyDark = () => document.documentElement.classList.add('dark')\n
 let applyLight = () => document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark')\n
\n
 if (appearance === 'system') {\n
 let media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')\n
\n
 window.localStorage.removeItem('flux.appearance')\n
\n
 media.matches ? applyDark() : applyLight()\n
 } else if (appearance === 'dark') {\n
 window.localStorage.setItem('flux.appearance', 'dark')\n
\n
 applyDark()\n
 } else if (appearance === 'light') {\n
 window.localStorage.setItem('flux.appearance', 'light')\n
\n
 applyLight()\n
 }\n
 }\n
 }\n
\n
 window.Flux.applyAppearance(window.localStorage.getItem('flux.appearance') || 'system')\n
</script>\n

 \n
 <div x-data="{\n
 init() {\n
 this.$nextTick(() => {\n
 if (typeof gsap === 'undefined') return;\n
\n
 const original = this.$refs.originalText;\n
 const warning = this.$refs.warningText;\n
\n
 gsap.set(warning, { opacity: 0 });\n
\n
 const tl = gsap.timeline({ paused: true });\n
\n
 tl.to(original, {\n
 y: -20,\n
 opacity: 0,\n
 duration: 0.3,\n
 ease: 'power2.in',\n
 }, 0);\n
\n
 tl.fromTo(warning, { y: 20, opacity: 0 }, {\n
 y: 0,\n
 opacity: 1,\n
 duration: 0.4,\n
 ease: 'back.out(1.2)',\n
 },\n
 '-=0.15',\n
 );\n
\n
 this.$el.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => tl.play());\n
 this.$el.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => tl.reverse());\n
 });\n
 },\n
 }"\n
 class="relative cursor-default overflow-hidden text-sm text-zinc-500 dark:text-zinc-400 w-full max-w-xl"\n
 style="min-height: 5rem;">\n
